### 知乎用户 叶三 发表
    
关于 AlphaFold2 抢颜宁饭碗的这个事情，找到的一篇文章：

AlphaFold2 fails to predict protein fold switching

AlphaFold2 has revolutionized protein structure prediction by leveraging sequence information to rapidly model protein folds with [atomic-level accuracy](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=atomic-level+accuracy&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D). Nevertheless, previous work has shown that these predictions tend to be inaccurate for structurally heterogeneous proteins. To systematically assess factors that contribute to this inaccuracy, we tested AlphaFold2's performance on [98-fold-switching proteins](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=98-fold-switching+proteins&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D), which assume at least two distinct-yet-stable secondary and tertiary structures. Topological similarities were quantified between five predicted and two experimentally determined structures of each fold-switching protein. Overall, 94% of AlphaFold2 predictions captured one experimentally determined conformation but not the other. Despite these biased results, AlphaFold2's estimated confidences were moderate-to-high for 74% of fold-switching residues, a result that contrasts with overall low confidences for intrinsically disordered proteins, which are also structurally heterogeneous. To investigate factors contributing to this [disparity](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=disparity&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D), we quantified sequence variation within the multiple sequence alignments used to generate AlphaFold2's predictions of fold-switching and intrinsically disordered proteins. Unlike intrinsically disordered regions, whose sequence alignments show low conservation, fold-switching regions had conservation rates statistically similar to canonical single-fold proteins. Furthermore, intrinsically disordered regions had systematically lower prediction confidences than either fold-switching or single-fold proteins, regardless of sequence conservation. AlphaFold2's high prediction confidences for fold switchers indicate that it uses sophisticated pattern recognition to search for one most probable conformer rather than protein [biophysics](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=biophysics&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D) to model a protein's structural ensemble. Thus, it is not surprising that its predictions often fail for proteins whose properties are not fully apparent from solved [protein structures](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=protein+structures&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D). Our results emphasize the need to look at protein structure as an ensemble and suggest that systematic examination of fold-switching sequences may reveal propensities for multiple stable secondary and tertiary structures.

AlphaFold2 无法预测蛋白质折叠转换

AlphaFold2 通过利用[序列信息](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)以原子级精度快速[建模](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E5%BB%BA%E6%A8%A1&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)蛋白质折叠，彻底改变了蛋白质结构预测。然而，先前的研究表明，这些预测对于[结构异质性蛋白质](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%BB%93%E6%9E%84%E5%BC%82%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E8%9B%8B%E7%99%BD%E8%B4%A8&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)来说往往是不准确的。为了系统地评估导致这种不准确的因素，我们测试了 AlphaFold2 在 98 倍切换蛋白上的性能，这些蛋白假定至少两种不同但稳定的二级和三级结构。对每个折叠开关蛋白的五个预测结构和两个实验确定结构之间的拓扑相似性进行量化。总体而言，94% 的 [AlphaFold2 预测](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=AlphaFold2%E9%A2%84%E6%B5%8B&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)捕捉到了一种实验确定的构象，但没有捕捉到另一种构象。尽管这些有偏差的结果，但对于 74% 的折叠切换[残基](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%AE%8B%E5%9F%BA&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)，AlphaFold2 的估计置信度为中等至高，这一结果与内在无序蛋白质的总体低置信度形成了对比，这些蛋白质在结构上也是异质的。为了研究导致这种差异的因素，我们量化了用于生成 AlphaFold2 对折叠切换和内在无序蛋白质的预测的多重序列比对中的序列变化。与内在无序区不同，其序列比对显示出低保守性，[折叠切换区](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%8A%98%E5%8F%A0%E5%88%87%E6%8D%A2%E5%8C%BA&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)的保守性在统计学上与典型的单折叠蛋白相似。此外，无论序列保守性如何，内在无序区域的预测置信度系统地低于折叠切换或单折叠蛋白质。AlphaFold2 对[折叠切换器](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%8A%98%E5%8F%A0%E5%88%87%E6%8D%A2%E5%99%A8&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)的高预测置信度表明，它使用复杂的[模式识别](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%A8%A1%E5%BC%8F%E8%AF%86%E5%88%AB&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)来寻找一个最可能的一致性，而不是蛋白质[生物物理学](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E7%89%A9%E7%90%86%E5%AD%A6&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)来建模蛋白质的结构整体。因此，它的预测常常会失败，而这些蛋白质的性质并不能从已解决的蛋白质结构中完全显现出来，这也就不足为奇了。我们的结果强调了将蛋白质结构视为一个整体的必要性，并表明对[折叠切换序列](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E6%8A%98%E5%8F%A0%E5%88%87%E6%8D%A2%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2741753903%7D)的系统检查可能会揭示多种稳定的二级和三级结构的倾向。

从这篇文章来看，AlphaFold2 暂时没有从成果上抢科学家的饭碗，但是，由于潜力巨大，社会资源开始向它倾斜了，因此，非常有可能在不久得将来，本该拨给颜宁们的经费会拨给 AlphaFold2 这种人工智能，所以，因为预料到前途灰暗，颜宁才转换战场吧。

房价 - 6：1994-2022 年香港房价走势与租金回报率，租金回报率与月供为什么必须超越房贷利率与租金？
------------------------------------------------------

《[房价 - 5：21 个主要城市房价历年走势一览，二手房价格大面积回落意味着什么？](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//mp.weixin.qq.com/s%3F__biz%3DMzU1MjE5MDAzNw%3D%3D%26mid%3D2247489313%26idx%3D1%26sn%3Deee49bb9616289a66a33f70e4e8c8182%26chksm%3Dfb84be1bccf3370d30d5accb3a4fbfe53d9bf605e643e50a987815e6b93d209925a2032e70c4%26scene%3D21%23wechat_redirect)》  
《[香港、深圳、杭州各项经济数据对比，谁的风险更大？](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//mp.weixin.qq.com/s%3F__biz%3DMzU1MjE5MDAzNw%3D%3D%26mid%3D2247484398%26idx%3D1%26sn%3Dec0196c1c156e2d1300e5ed8951ac4cd%26chksm%3Dfb84aad4ccf323c2e785a00930b64f6322d9d682906f6e0d8fa48cb3a3fb670df198dd6e9544%26scene%3D21%23wechat_redirect)》  
《[汇率贬值是否能够保房价，从莫斯科房价谈起，为何 1990 年日本和 1998 年香港不选择贬值汇率保房价？](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//mp.weixin.qq.com/s%3F__biz%3DMzU1MjE5MDAzNw%3D%3D%26mid%3D2247487506%26idx%3D1%26sn%3Dfe4ab5498b0dc704eddc239015e3fcd1%26chksm%3Dfb84b928ccf3303e49a24e1eb9c779809e222c02cfe874a3d73b20f0f896be994ca8896cb702%26scene%3D21%23wechat_redirect)》  
《[从 1997 年香港存贷数据，看杭州存贷比的极限](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//mp.weixin.qq.com/s%3F__biz%3DMzU1MjE5MDAzNw%3D%3D%26mid%3D2247484374%26idx%3D1%26sn%3D77bab62c1f00c16c02d8f5baff2fc082%26chksm%3Dfb84aaecccf323fad621b8e24848f38466ab6b949adfffda7d2f21496a5da3f99c401b3c8733%26scene%3D21%23wechat_redirect)》  
《[香港 - 全球经济 - 通胀式复苏与泡沫共存](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//mp.weixin.qq.com/s%3F__biz%3DMzU1MjE5MDAzNw%3D%3D%26mid%3D2247485446%26idx%3D1%26sn%3D6db9cccc733da9acd0027ebedface440%26chksm%3Dfb84a13cccf3282ac5852a5821bc617792bb3c07dc55daf82cfef6a48e56acb8bddd86c835b2%26scene%3D21%23wechat_redirect)》  

![](https://images.weserv.nl/?url=https%3A//pic1.zhimg.com/v2-46e2761ec3d6685d1b68f46e77cdf39e_r.jpg%3Fsource%3D1940ef5c)

![](https://images.weserv.nl/?url=https%3A//pica.zhimg.com/v2-0eb24e19fd8d625e926decee230ee9be_r.jpg%3Fsource%3D1940ef5c)

![](https://images.weserv.nl/?url=https%3A//picx1.zhimg.com/v2-6541681d0104c49221ea5b01d77519bc_r.jpg%3Fsource%3D1940ef5c)

![](https://images.weserv.nl/?url=https%3A//picx1.zhimg.com/v2-359dd7308f190f60b3035d7d038ce93d_r.jpg%3Fsource%3D1940ef5c)

  
香港房贷利率为 2.4%，香港租金回报率为 2.62%，即租金回报率大于房贷利率，但从收租的交易来看，在香港买房是非常划算的。  
大陆一线、二线、三线的租金回报率很低，大部分地区租金回报率位于 1.5%-2.5%，而房贷利率基本在 5% 左右，房贷利率远大于实际商品房收益率，那么未来显而易见的事情是房贷利率无限的接近于 2%，那也无法阻挡租金回报率太低的事实，如果房价下跌 50%，租金下跌 30%，那么**租金回报率将上升至 2.1%-3.5%**。  
因此大陆房价必然要经历 50% 的回落，北京、上海房价可能回到 3w / 平下方，二线热点城市房价必然回落至 7k / 平以内（**以租金收益角度估值**）。  
从 1994-2022 年香港房价走势来看，房价与失业率呈现反比关系，随着失业率的上升房价必然回落。  

![](https://images.weserv.nl/?url=https%3A//picx1.zhimg.com/v2-ffc52683bd86865001aac79d0b527c22_r.jpg%3Fsource%3D1940ef5c)

  
将**香港数据与韩国对比，韩国的居民杠杆率更高，商品房泡沫程度越高**，韩国 50% 的人口都集中在[首尔都市区](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E9%A6%96%E5%B0%94%E9%83%BD%E5%B8%82%E5%8C%BA&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2740949265%7D)，类似于陕西三分之一的人口集中在西安，这种人口分布会导致其他地市和区域极度贫困，本身一定会导致内卷加剧、贫富差距加大、[生育率](https://www.zhihu.com/search?q=%E7%94%9F%E8%82%B2%E7%8E%87&search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_source=Entity&hybrid_search_extra=%7B%22sourceType%22%3A%22answer%22%2C%22sourceId%22%3A2740949265%7D)降低。  
[\[1\]]()

![](https://images.weserv.nl/?url=https%3A//pica.zhimg.com/v2-44c1fa960c85cb6d4b81bc4a9e519071_r.jpg%3Fsource%3D1940ef5c)

强省会、弱地市、强一线、弱二线一定会导致畸形的房价、教育、生育、社会价值观。
